### Post by luc4 on 2014-10-05
Hi,
I just got a old laptop, installed my favorite OS(Ubuntu 14.04 LTS) on it.;)
But I can't get[*****bluetooth*]("https://www.google.nl/search?client=ubuntu&hs=pHU&channel=fs&q=bluetooth&spell=1&sa=X&ei=aloxVI_fHsrYPIafgPgD&ved=0CCEQvwUoAA") working?
any tips on switching bluetoth on and letting the sys regognise?
Greetins,
Luc

---

### Post by tgalati4 on 2014-10-05
Open a terminal and post the output of:

```
lspci
lsusb
```

### Post by Vladlenin5000 on 2014-10-05
A quick search suggests the Bluetooth for that model is an optional. Most reviews don't even mention it but there are drivers for a Broadcom Bluetooth at Acer's.

I suspect the Bluetooth was included in models with a companion Broadcom WiFi only. Models delivered with Intel or Atheros WiFi (yours) most likely didn't have that option. Granted, unless working from a single hybrid chip, BT and WiFi are independent. However, back on 2006-7, if I were to build or just design a machine like that I would put Broadcom with Broadcom just to get the least theoretical possibilities of conflits or interference.

---

### Post by Vladlenin5000 on 2014-10-05
> **luc4 said:**
> but why do i then see the bluetooth button and light, the person who gave it to me said that it had bluetooth?

That's what optional means... you can add it later.
Have you seen it working with other OS?
The fact remains it isn't being detected so, most likely it's either absent or faulty.
